				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Bleib bei uns, denn es will Abend werden, BWV 6 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1725; rev. 1727; 1736/1740
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Sacred_cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Sacred cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Cantatas&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Cantatas</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Religious_works&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Religious works</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="16 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_4_voices%2C_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 4 voices, mixed chorus, orchestra</a></span>; <td>IJB 42

</th>
<td>C minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>6 movements:
<ol><li> Chorus: Bleib bei uns, denn es will Abend werden (C&#160;minor)
</li><li> Aria (alto): Hochgelobter Gottessohn (E<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Chorale (soprano): Ach bleib bei uns, Herr Jesu Christ (B<span class="music-symbol" style="font-family: Arial Unicode MS, Lucida Sans Unicode; font-size:110%">&#x266d;</span>&#160;major)
</li><li> Recitative (bass): Es hat die Dunkelheit an vielen Orten (G&#160;minor)
</li><li> Aria (tenor): Jesu, laß uns auf dich sehen (G&#160;minor)
</li><li> Chorale: Beweis dein Macht, Herr Jesu Christ (G&#160;minor)
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
